provided plan, the medical and dental</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>7</font></p><br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>benefits provided by the Company under this Plan shall be secondary to those provided under such other plan during the applicable period of eligibility; </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iv)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>for two years after the Date of Termination in the case of a Schedule A Participant or three years after the Date of Termination in the case of a Schedule B Participant (or such longer period as may be provided by the terms of the appropriate plan, program, practice or policy), the Company shall continue benefits (other than medical and dental benefits, but including financial planning assistance) to the Participant and/or the Participant&#146;s family at least equal to those which would have been provided to them in accordance with the welfare plans, programs, practices and policies maintained by the Company if the Participant&#146;s employment had not been terminated or, if more favorable to the Participant, as in effect generally at any time thereafter with respect to other peer executives of the Employer
and their families; </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(v)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>the Participant&#146;s eligibility (but not the time of commencement of such benefits) for retiree benefits pursuant to the welfare plans, programs, practices and policies maintained by the Company shall be determined as if the Participant had (A) remained employed until two years (in the case of a Schedule A Participant) or three years (in the case of a Schedule B Participant) after the Date of Termination and (B) retired on the last day of such period; </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(vi)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>the Participant shall be paid, in a lump sum payment in cash, an amount equal to the excess of: </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(A)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>the actuarial equivalent of the benefit under the Company&#146;s applicable qualified defined benefit retirement plan in which the Participant is participating immediately prior to his Date of Termination (the &#147;Retirement Plan&#148;) (utilizing the rate used to determine lump sums and, to the extent applicable, other actuarial assumptions no less favorable to the Participant than those in effect under the Retirement Plan immediately prior to the Effective Date), any supplemental executive retirement plans (&#147;SERPs&#148;) in which the Participant participates and, to the extent applicable, any other defined benefit retirement arrangement between the Participant and the Company (&#147;Other Pension Benefits&#148;) which the Participant would receive if the Participant&#146;s employment continued for
two or three additional years (for Schedule A Participants and Schedule B Participants, respectively) beyond the Date of Termination and, assuming that the Participant&#146;s compensation for such deemed additional period was the Participant&#146;s Annual Base Salary as in effect immediately prior to the Date of Termination and assuming a bonus in each year during such deemed additional period equal to the Target Bonus, over</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(B)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>the actuarial equivalent of the Participant&#146;s actual benefit (paid or payable), if any, under the Retirement Plan, the SERPs and Other Pension Benefits as of the Date of Termination (utilizing the rate used to determine lump sums and, to the extent applicable, other actuarial assumptions no less favorable</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>8</font></p><br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><PAGE>




 <p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>to the Participant than those in effect under the Retirement Plan immediately prior to the effective date of the Change in Control);</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(vii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>any compensation previously deferred (other than pursuant to a tax-qualified plan) by or on behalf of the Participant (together with any accrued interest or earnings thereon), whether or not then vested, shall become vested on the Date of Termination and shall be paid in accordance with the terms of the plan, policy or practice under which it was deferred to the extent permitted by guidance issued by the U.S. Department of Treasury under Section 409A of the Code;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(viii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>the Company shall, at its sole expense as incurred, provide the Participant with outplacement services suitable to the Participant&#146;s position for a period not to exceed one year following the Date of Termination with a nationally recognized outplacement firm; and,</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(ix)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>to the extent not theretofore paid or provided, the Company shall pay or provide to the Participant any other amounts or benefits required to be paid or provided or which the Participant is entitled to receive under any plan, program, policy, practice, contract or agreement of the Company (or other Employer), including earned but unpaid stock and similar compensation, but excluding medical or dental benefits if the Participant is eligible for such benefits to be provided by a subsequent employer, and benefits payable under any severance plan or policy (such other amounts and benefits that are payable to the Participant shall be hereinafter referred to as the &#147;Other Benefits&#148;).</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>4.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk32">Termination By Employer For Cause or By Participant Other Than For Good Reason</a></font></u><font size=2>. If, at any time after a Change in Control, either (a) an Employer shall terminate a Participant&#146;s employment for Cause or (b) the Participant shall voluntarily terminate his employment other than for Good Reason, the Employer shall have no further payment obligations to the Participant other than for amounts described in Sections 4.1(i)(A)(1) and 4.1(i)(A)(3) and the timely payment or provision of Other Benefits. In such case, all such amounts shall be paid to the Participant in a lump sum.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>4.3</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk33">Death</a></font></u><font size=2>. If a Participant&#146;s employment terminates by reason of the Participant&#146;s death after a Change in Control, all Accrued Obligations as of the time of death shall be paid to the Participant&#146;s estate or beneficiary, as applicable, in a lump sum in cash and the Participant&#146;s estate or beneficiary shall be entitled to any Other Benefits in accordance with their terms. Any Prior Equity Awards shall vest and/or become exercisable, as the case may be, as of the Date of Termination and the Participant&#146;s estate or beneficiary, as the case may be, shall have the right to exercise any such Prior Equity Award until the earlier of (a) one year from the Date of Termination (or such longer period as may be provided under the terms of any such Prior Equity Award)
and (b) the normal expiration date of such Prior Equity Award.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>4.4</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk34">Disability</a></font></u><font size=2>. If a Participant&#146;s employment is terminated by reason of Disability after a Change in Control, all Accrued Obligations shall be paid to the Participant in a lump sum in cash and the Participant&#146;s estate or beneficiary shall be entitled to any Other Benefits in accordance with their terms.  Any Prior Equity Awards shall vest immediately and/or become exercisable, as the case may be, and the Participant shall have the right to exercise any such Prior </font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>9</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>Equity Award until the earlier of (a) one year from the Date of Termination (or such longer period as may be provided under the terms of any such Prior Equity Award) and (b) the normal expiration date of such Prior Equity Award.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>4.5</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk35">Retirement</a></font></u><font size=2>. If a Participant&#146;s employment terminates as a result of Retirement after a Change in Control, the Participant shall be paid the Accrued Obligations in a lump sum in cash and the Participant shall be entitled to any Other Benefits in accordance with their terms.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ARTICLE V</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>TIMING
  OF, LIMITATIONS ON AND ADJUSTMENTS TO PLAN PAYMENTS</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>5.1</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk36">Time of Payments</a></font></u><font size=2>. Payments under the Plan shall be made as soon as practicable after the Participant&#146;s Date of Termination, except, however, that any payment that is subject to the requirements of Section 409A of the Code shall be made as soon as practicable after the earlier of (i) the six-month anniversary of the Participant&#146;s Date of Termination (other than by reason of death) and (ii) the date of the Participant&#146;s death.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>5.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk37">Payment Offsets</a></font></u><font size=2>. Notwithstanding anything in the Plan to the contrary, in the event a Participant is entitled to receive severance payments both under this Plan and under the terms of either (i) an individual change of control or employment agreement, (ii) another severance pay plan or policy of an Employer or (iii) any existing or future law or regulation, the benefits payable under this Plan shall be reduced by the amount of any severance benefits such Participant is entitled to receive under such individual agreement, plan, policy, law or regulation.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>5.3</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk38">Cap on Excess Parachute Payments; Gross-Up Payments</a></font></u><font size=2>. Notwithstanding anything in the Plan to the contrary, if (i) a Participant is a &#147;disqualified individual&#148; (as defined in Section 280G(c) of the Code) and (ii) the severance benefits provided under Articles IV or V, together with any other payments the Participant has the right to receive from an Employer, would constitute a &#147;parachute payment&#148; (as defined in Section 280G(b) of the Code) (&#147;Parachute Payments&#148;), the following provisions shall apply:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(a)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Schedule A Participants</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(i)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>In the case of a Schedule A Participant, the severance benefits under Article IV shall not exceed an amount which, together with any other Parachute Payments the Participant has a right to receive from the Employer, would be 2.99 times the Participant&#146;s &#147;base amount&#148; (as defined in Section 280G of the Code) so that no portion of the amounts received by the Participant shall be subject to the excise tax imposed under Section 4999 of the Code.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(ii) </font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>The determination of whether any limitation on the severance benefits payable under Article IV is necessary shall be made by the Company&#146;s independent auditor or such other certified public accounting firm as may be jointly</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>10</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>designated by the Participant and the Company (the &#147;Accounting Firm&#148;), which shall provide detailed supporting calculations to the Participant and the Company. The determinations of the Accounting Firm shall be conclusive and binding on the Company and the Participant.  All fees and expenses of the Accounting Firm shall be borne solely by the Company.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>If through error or otherwise a Schedule A Participant shall receive payments under the Plan, together with other Parachute Payments the Participant has the right to receive from an Employer, in excess of 2.99 times his base amount, the Participant shall immediately repay the excess to the Employer upon notification from the Employer that an overpayment has been made. If the Participant fails to repay the excess to the Employer within 10 business days of the date of the Employer&#146;s notification, the Participant will become liable to the Employer for an amount equal to two (2) times the excess amount.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(b)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Schedule B Participants</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(i)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>In the event it shall be determined that any severance benefits payable to a Schedule B Participant under Articles IV (together with any other Parachute Payments the Participant has a right to receive from the Employer) would be subject to the excise tax imposed by Section 4999 of the Code or any interest or penalties are incurred by the Participant with respect to such excise tax (such excise tax, together with any such interest and penalties, are hereinafter collectively referred to as the &#147;Excise Tax&#148;), then the Participant shall be entitled to receive an additional payment (a &#147;Gross-Up Payment&#148;) in an amount such that after payment by the Participant of all taxes (including any interest or penalties imposed with respect to such taxes), including, without limitation,
any income and employment taxes (and any interest and penalties imposed with respect thereto) and Excise Tax imposed upon the Gross-Up Payment, the Participant retains an amount of the Gross-Up Payment equal to the Excise Tax imposed upon the Parachute Payments.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(ii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Subject to the provisions of Section 5.2(b)(iii), all determinations required to be made under this Section 5.2(b), including whether and when a Gross-Up Payment is required and the amount of such Gross-Up Payment and the assumptions to be utilized in arriving at such determination, shall be made by the Accounting Firm, which shall provide detailed supporting calculations to the Participant and the Company. All fees and expenses of the Accounting Firm shall be borne solely by the Company. Any Gross-Up Payment, as determined pursuant to this Section 5.2(b), shall be paid by the Company to the Participant as soon as practicable after the receipt of the Accounting Firm&#146;s determination. Any determination by the Accounting Firm shall be binding upon the Participant and the Company. As a result of
the uncertainty in the application of Section 4999 of the Code at the time of the initial determination by the Accounting Firm hereunder, it is possible that Gross-Up Payments which will not have been made by the Company should have been made (&#147;Underpayment&#148;), consistent with the calculations required to be made hereunder. In the event that the Company exhausts its remedies pursuant to Section 5.2(b)(iii) and the Participant thereafter is required to make a payment of any Excise Tax, the Accounting Firm shall determine the amount of the </font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>11</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>Underpayment that has occurred and any such Underpayment shall be promptly paid by the Company to or for the benefit of the Participant.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>A Schedule B Participant shall notify the Company in writing of any claim by the Internal Revenue Service that, if successful, would require the payment by the Company of the Gross-Up Payment. Such notification shall be given as soon as practicable but no later than ten business days after the Participant is informed in writing of such claim and shall apprise the Company of the nature of such claim and the date on which such claim is requested to be paid. The Participant shall not pay such claim prior to the expiration of the 30-day period following the date on which he gives such notice to the Company (or such shorter period ending on the date that any payment of taxes with respect to such claim is due). If the Company notifies the Participant in writing prior to the expiration of such period that it
desires to contest such claim, the Participant shall:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; text-indent:1.08in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(A)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>give the Company any information reasonably requested by the Company relating to such claim,</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; text-indent:1.08in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(B)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>take such action in connection with contesting such claim as the Company shall reasonably request in writing from time to time, including, without limitation, accepting legal representation with respect to such claim by an attorney reasonably selected by the Company,</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; text-indent:1.08in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(C)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>cooperate with the Company in good faith in order effectively to contest such claim, and</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.72in; text-indent:1.08in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(D)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>permit the Company to participate in any proceedings relating to such claim;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>provided however, that the Company shall bear and pay directly all costs and expenses (including additional interest and penalties) incurred in connection with such contest and shall indemnify and hold the Participant harmless, on an after-tax basis, for any Excise Tax or income tax (including interest and penalties with respect thereto) imposed as a result of such representation and payment of costs and expenses. Without limitation on the foregoing provisions of this Section 5.2(b)(iii), the Company shall control all proceedings taken in connection with such contest and, at its sole option, may pursue or forgo any and all administrative appeals, proceedings, hearings and conferences with the taxing authority in respect of such claim and may, at its sole option, either direct the Participant to pay the tax claimed and sue for a refund or contest the claim in any permissible manner, and the Participant
agrees to prosecute such contest to a determination before any administrative tribunal, in a court of initial jurisdiction and in one or more appellate courts, as the Company shall determine; provided however, that if the Company directs the Participant to pay such claim and sue for a refund, the Company shall advance the amount of such payment to the Participant, on an interest-free basis and shall indemnify and hold the Participant harmless, on an after-tax basis, from any Excise Tax or income tax (including interest or penalties with respect thereto) imposed with respect to such advance or with respect to any imputed income with respect to such</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>12</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>advance; and further provided that any extension of the statute of limitations relating to payment of taxes for the taxable year of the Participant with respect to which such contested amount is claimed to be due is limited solely to such contested amount. Furthermore, the Company&#146;s control of the contest shall be limited to issues with respect to which a Gross-Up Payment would be payable hereunder and the Participant shall be entitled to settle or contest, as the case may be, any other issue raised by the Internal Revenue Service or any other taxing authority.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iv)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>If, after the receipt by a Schedule B Participant of an amount advanced by the Company pursuant to Section 5.2(b)(iii), the Participant becomes entitled to receive any refund with respect to such claim, the Participant shall (subject to the Company&#146;s complying with the requirements of Section 5.2(b)(iii)) promptly pay to the Company the amount of such refund (together with any interest paid or credited thereon after taxes applicable thereto). If, after the receipt by the Participant of an amount advanced by the Company pursuant to Section 5.2(b)(iii), a determination is made that the Participant shall not be entitled to any refund with respect to such claim and the Company does not notify the Participant in writing of its intent to contest such denial of refund prior to the expiration of 30 days after
such determination, then such advance shall be forgiven and shall not be required to be repaid and the amount of such advance shall offset, to the extent thereof, the amount of Gross-Up Payment required to be paid.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>5.4</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk39">Code Section 409A Compliance</a></font></u><font size=2>. Notwithstanding anything in the Plan to the contrary, all Plan benefit obligations and payments are subject to guidance issued by the U.S. Department of Treasury under Section 409A of the Code. To the extent required, the Company may modify the severance benefits payable hereunder to comply with such guidance; provided, however, that the present value of the aggregate Plan benefits payable to a Participant after such modification shall not be less than the present value of the Plan benefits payable to the Participant prior to the modification.   </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>5.5</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk40">Tax Withholding</a></font></u><font size=2>. Notwithstanding any other provision of this Plan, the Company may withhold from any amounts payable under this Plan such Federal, state, local or foreign taxes as shall be required to be withheld pursuant to any applicable law or regulation.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ARTICLE VI</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>RESTRICTIVE COVENANTS</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>6.1</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk41">Confidentiality</a></font></u><font size=2>. As a condition to participation in the Plan, each Participant agrees to hold in a fiduciary capacity for the benefit of the Company and its Affiliates all Confidential Information which shall have been obtained by the Participant during the Participant&#146;s employment by the Employer; except, however, that this Section 6.1 shall not apply to Confidential Information that is or becomes public knowledge, unless such Confidential Information became or becomes public knowledge due to acts of the  Participant or representatives of the Participant in violation of this Section 6.1. Upon termination of the</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>13</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>Participant&#146;s employment, he shall return to the Company all Confidential Information in his possession. After termination of the Participant&#146;s employment with the Employer, the Participant shall not, without the prior written consent of the Company or as may otherwise be required by law or legal process, communicate or divulge any such Confidential Information to anyone other than the Company and those designated by it, except (x) otherwise publicly available information, (y) as may be necessary to enforce his rights under the Plan or as necessary to defend himself against a claim asserted directly or indirectly by the Company or its Affiliates; or (z) as may be compelled by service of a valid subpoena or other legal process. If the Participant is served with a valid subpoena or other legal process, he must so notify the Company within three business days. Unless and until a determination has been made in
accordance with Section 6.4 that the Participant has violated this Section 6.1, an asserted violation of the provisions of this Section 6.1 shall not constitute a basis for deferring or withholding any amounts otherwise payable to the Participant under the Plan. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>6.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk42">Non-Compete</a></font></u><font size=2>. As a condition to participation in the Plan, each Participant agrees, that, in the event the Participant voluntarily terminates his employment other than for Good Reason, for the period of one year from Date of Termination he will not, without the written consent of the Company, directly or indirectly own, manage, operate, join, control, become employed by, consult to or participate in the ownership, management, or control of any business which is in direct competition with the Company or its Affiliates. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>6.3</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk43">Non-Solicitation</a></font></u><font size=2>. As a condition to participation in the Plan, each Participant agrees that, in the event the Participant voluntarily terminates his employment other than for Good Reason, for the period of one year following the Date of Termination, he will not, directly or indirectly, solicit or hire, or encourage the solicitation or hiring by any employer other than the Company or its Affiliates, for any position as an employee, independent contractor, consultant or otherwise, any person who was a managerial or higher level employee of an Employer at any time during the term of the Participant&#146;s employment by the Employer; provided, however, that this provision shall not apply with respect to the solicitation of any person after six months from the date on which such
person&#146;s employment by an Employer has terminated.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>6.4</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk44">Enforcement</a></font></u><font size=2>. In the event of a breach by the Participant of any of the covenants set forth in this Article VI, it is agreed that the Company shall suffer irreparable harm for which money damages are not an adequate remedy, and that, in the event of such breach, the Company shall be entitled to obtain an order of a court of competent jurisdiction for equitable relief from such breach, including, but not limited to, temporary restraining orders and preliminary and/or permanent injunctions against the breach of such covenants by the Participant. In the event that the Company should initiate any legal action for the breach or enforcement of any of the provisions contained in this Article VI and the Company does not prevail in such action, the Company shall promptly reimburse the
Participant the full amount of any court costs, filing fees, attorney&#146;s fees which the Participant incurs in defending such action, and any loss of income during the period of such litigation.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'>14</p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ARTICLE VII</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>AMENDMENT AND TERMINATION</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>7.1</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk45">Amendment</a></font></u><font size=2>. The Company may amend this Plan at any time, and from time to time, by action of the Committee; provided, however, that no amendment adopted after the effective date of a Change in Control shall have the effect of either (i) removing an individual from the list of Participants, (ii) adding conditions for participation or the entitlement to receive benefits hereunder, (iii) reducing the amount of benefits payable to a Participant or (iv) otherwise restricting a Participant&#146;s right to receive benefits under the Plan, except as may otherwise be required to conform such payments to the requirements of Section 409A of the Code, as provided in Section 1.1.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>7.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk46">Termination</a></font></u><font size=2>. The Committee may terminate the Plan at any time prior to a Change in Control. The Plan may not be terminated after the effective date of a Change in Control, except that the Plan shall automatically terminate on the 24-month anniversary of a Change in Control, except with respect to benefits payable on and after the date of termination.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ARTICLE VIII</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ADMINISTRATION</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.1</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk47">Plan Administrator</a></font></u><font size=2>. The Plan shall be administered by the Committee, which shall have the duties and responsibilities for administering the Plan as are specifically set forth in this Article VIII. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk48">Responsibilities of Committee</a></font></u><font size=2>. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(a)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>The Committee shall have responsibility for the day to day administration of the Plan. In addition, the Committee shall the specific powers, duties, responsibilities and obligations specifically provided for herein.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(b)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Subject to the express provisions of the Plan, the Committee shall have full and exclusive authority to interpret the Plan and to make all other factual determinations deemed necessary or advisable in the implementation and administration of the Plan, including but not limited to determinations with respect to the eligibility of Participants to receive benefits under the Plan and the status and rights of such Participants and all other persons affected hereunder. The Committee&#146;s interpretation and construction of the Plan shall be conclusive and binding on all persons. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(c)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>The Committee shall have sole authority to adopt rules and regulations, which shall be administered by the Committee. In addition, the Committee shall have the discretionary authority to issue rulings and interpretations concerning the Plan and all matters arising thereunder, on a uniform and nondiscriminatory basis, provided the same shall not be contrary to or inconsistent with any provision of the Plan.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>15</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(d)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>As a condition of distributing any benefit under the Plan, the Committee may prescribe the use of such forms and require the furnishing of such information as the Plan Committee may deem appropriate for administering the Plan.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.3</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk49">Allocation or Delegation of Duties and Responsibilities</a></font></u><font size=2>. In furtherance of its duties and responsibilities under the Plan, the Committee may,</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(a)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Employ agents to carry out non-fiduciary responsibilities;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(b)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Employ agents to carry out fiduciary responsibilities;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(c)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Consult with counsel, who may be counsel to the Company; and </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(d)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Delegate any of its duties and responsibilities hereunder to such officer or officers of the Company as the Committee shall designate; except, however, that the Committee may not delegate to any other person the designation of Eligible Employees under Section 3.1.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.4</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk50">Expenses</a></font></u><font size=2>. Unless otherwise agreed to by the Company, no person acting as a fiduciary hereunder (who is an employee of an Employer) shall receive any compensation for services as such. Expenses incurred by fiduciaries in connection with the administration of the Plan shall be paid by the Company.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.5</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk51">Indemnification of Plan Administrator</a></font></u><font size=2>. The Company shall indemnify, to the fullest extent permitted by law, each person made or threatened to be made a party to any civil or criminal action or proceeding by reason of the fact that he, or his testator or intestate, was a member of the Committee, or a delegate of the Committee, acting in the capacity of Plan administrator.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.6</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk52">Reliance Upon Others</a></font></u><font size=2>. The Committee, any person to whom it may delegate such of its duties and powers as provided herein, and the officers and directors of the Company shall be entitled to rely conclusively upon and shall be fully protected in any action taken by them in good faith in reliance upon any tables, valuations, certificates, opinions, reports or other advice furnished to them by any duly appointed actuary, accountant, legal counsel (who may be counsel for the Company) or other specialist.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.7</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk53">Notification</a></font></u><font size=2>. All notices, reports and statements in connection with the Plan that are given, made, delivered or transmitted to a Participant shall be deemed duly given, made, delivered, or transmitted when mailed, by such class as the sender may deem appropriate, with postage prepaid and addressed to the Participant at the address last appearing on the records of the Employer with respect to this Plan. All notices, direct actions or other communications given, made, delivered or transmitted by a Participant to an Employer or Committee shall not be deemed to have been duly given, made, delivered, transmitted or received unless and until actually received by the Employer or Committee.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>8.8</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk54">Multiple Capacities</a></font></u><font size=2>. A person may serve in more than one fiduciary capacity with respect to the Plan.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>16</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ARTICLE IX</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>CLAIMS PROCEDURE</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>9.1</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk55">Submission of Claims</a></font></u><font size=2>. The initial claim by any Participant for benefits under this Plan shall be submitted in writing to the Committee within 60 days after the occurrence of the termination of employment that the Participant claims to have triggered entitlement to Plan benefits.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>9.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk56">Computation and Review of Claims</a></font></u><font size=2>. All benefits shall be computed by the Committee or its delegate. All claims shall be approved or denied by the Committee (or its delegate) as soon as practicable, but in no event later than 90 days after application by the claimant.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(a)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><i><font size=2>Initial Denial of Claim</font></i><font size=2>&#151;Any denial of a claim shall include:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(i)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Reason or reasons for the denial;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(ii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Reference to pertinent Plan provisions on which the denial is based;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Description of any additional material or information necessary for the claimant to perfect the claim together with an explanation of why the material or information is necessary; and</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iv)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Explanation of the Plan&#146;s claim review procedure, described below.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(b)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><i><font size=2>Review of a Denied Claim</font></i><font size=2>&#151;A claimant shall have a reasonable opportunity to appeal a denied claim to the Committee (or its delegate) for a full and fair review. The claimant or a duly authorized representative:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(i)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Shall have 60 days, after receipt of written notification of the denial of claim in which to request a review.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(ii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>May request a review upon written application to the Committee.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Shall submit written comments, documents, records and other information relating to the claim.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iv)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>May review, free of charge, pertinent Plan documents, records and other information relevant to the claim.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(c)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><i><font size=2>Committee Review</font></i><font size=2>&#151;The Committee&#146;s (or its delegate&#146;s) review shall take into account all comments, documents, records and other information submitted by the claimant relating to the claim, without regard to whether such information was submitted or considered in the initial benefit determination.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>17</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(d)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><i><font size=2>Written Decision</font></i><font size=2>&#151;The Committee (or its delegate) shall issue a decision on the reviewed claim promptly but no later than 60 days after receipt of the review. The Committee&#146;s decision shall be in writing and shall include:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(i)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Reasons for the decision, </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(ii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>References to the Plan provisions on which the decision is based, and</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:0.36in; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(iii)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Statement that the claimant is entitled to receive, upon request, reasonable access to, and copies of, all documents, records and other information relevant to the claim</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(e)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><i><font size=2>Binding Effect</font></i><font size=2>&#151;The Committee&#146;s (or its delegate&#146;s) decision shall be final and binding on the claimant and the Employer.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>ARTICLE X </font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><font SIZE=2>GENERAL PROVISIONS</font></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.1</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk57">Construction</a></font></u><font size=2>. This Plan shall be construed and enforced in accordance with and governed by the internal substantive laws (and not the laws relating to conflict of laws or choice of laws) of the State of New Jersey, except to the extent that such laws are preempted by Federal law.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.2</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk58">Unfunded Plan</a></font></u><font size=2>. The obligations of the Company under this Plan are not required to be funded in advance. Nothing contained in this Plan shall give an Eligible Employee or Participant any right, title or interest in any property of the Company or any of its Affiliates.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10. </font><a name="bk59"></a><font size=2>3</font><u><font size=2></font></u><font size=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>No Right to Continued Employment</font></u><font size=2>. Nothing contained herein shall be deemed to give any Eligible Employee or Participant the right to be retained in the employment of an Employer or to limit the rights of any Employer to discharge any Eligible Employee or Participant at any time, with or without notice and with or without Cause.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.4</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk60">Partial Invalidity</a></font></u><font size=2>. The invalidity or unenforceability of any term or provision, or any clause, or portion thereof, of this Plan shall in no way impair or affect the validity or enforceability of any other provision of this Plan, which shall remain in full force and effect.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.5</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk61">Successors and Assigns</a></font></u><font size=2>.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Plan shall inure to the benefit of and be binding upon the Company and its successors and assigns.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(b)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>The Company shall require any successor (whether direct or indirect, by purchase, merger, consolidation or otherwise) to all or substantially all of the business and/or assets of the Company to assume expressly and agree to perform the Company&#146;s obligations under the Plan in the same manner and to the same extent that the Company would be required to perform it if no such succession had taken place.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>18</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.72in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>(c)</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>In no event shall a Participant assign his interests under the Plan to any other person without the prior written consent of the Committee. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.6</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk62">Waivers</a></font></u><font size=2>. Failure to strictly comply with any term, condition or requirement set forth in the Plan shall not be deemed a waiver of such term, condition or requirement, nor shall any waiver of any such term, condition or requirement at any one time or times be deemed to result in a waiver of such term, condition or requirement at any other time or times.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.7</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk63">Gender and Number</a></font></u><font size=2>. Masculine pronouns include the feminine as well as the neuter genders, and the singular shall include the plural, unless indicated otherwise by the context.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>10.8</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2><a name="bk64">Headings</a></font></u><font size=2>. The headings of the Plan are for purposes of reference only and shall not limit or otherwise affect the meaning hereof.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>19</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>

<td width="15" valign=top > <p style='margin-top:2pt;margin-bottom:0pt;' ><font size=1>&nbsp;</font></p> </td>
<td width="107" valign=bottom > <p style='margin-top:2pt;margin-bottom:0pt;' ><font size=1>&nbsp;</font></p> </td> </tr> </table>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'>&nbsp;</p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><b><font SIZE=2>EXHIBIT I</font></b></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><b><font size=2>Form of Restrictive Covenant Agreement</font></b></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>AGREEMENT,
  by and between Public Service Enterprise Group Incorporated, a New Jersey Corporation
  (the &#147;Company&#148;) and [ _________________ ] (&#147;Executive&#148;),
  dated as of [ ______________ ].</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, the Company maintains the Key Executive Severance Plan of Public Service Enterprise Group Incorporated (the &#147;Plan&#148;), effective December 20, 2004, and as thereafter amended, modified or supplemented;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, Executive was designated as an Eligible Employee under the Plan by the Organization and Compensation Committee of the Company&#146;s board of directors on December 19, 2004;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, pursuant to Section 3.2 of the Plan, in order to be a Participant in and be entitled to benefits and protections under the Plan, Executive must execute and delivery to the Company within 30 days after Executive was designated as an Eligible Employee a written agreement to be bound by the terms and conditions of certain covenants set out in Article VI of the Plan, which is hereby incorporated herein; </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>NOW THEREFORE, the parties agree as follows:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>1.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Executive has received a copy of the Plan and has read and understands the terms of conditions of Section 6.1, </font><u><font size=2>Confidentiality</font></u><font size=2>, Section 6.2, </font><u><font size=2>Non-Compete</font></u><font size=2>, and Section 6.3, </font><u><font size=2>Non-Solicitation</font></u><font size=2>, therein, as applied to Executive (the &#147;Covenants&#148;).</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>2.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Executive agrees to be bound by and comply with the terms of the Covenants in consideration for becoming a Participant in the Plan. </font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>3.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Executive acknowledges that the Covenants are reasonable in the scope of the activities restricted, the geographic area covered by the restrictions, the duration of the restrictions, and that such Covenants are reasonably necessary to protect the Company&#146;s legitimate interests in its Confidential Information and its relationships with its employees, customers and suppliers.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>4.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Executive acknowledges that the Covenants will not deprive Executive of the ability to earn a livelihood or to support Executive&#146;s dependents.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>5.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>Executive shall be a Participant in the Plan and be entitled to all of the rights and benefits provided thereunder as of the date of this Agreement.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>6.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font size=2>This Agreement shall be construed and enforced in accordance with and governed by the internal substantive laws (and not the laws relating to conflict of laws or choice of laws) of the State of New Jersey, except to the extent that such laws are preempted by Federal law.</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'>&nbsp;</p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the parties have executed this Agreement as of the date and year first above written.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>[This Agreement may be executed in counterparts.]</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt;'><font size=2>&nbsp;</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>2</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><b><font SIZE=2>EXHIBIT II</font></b></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center; margin-top:16pt;'><u><b><font size=2>Form of Separation Agreement and General Release</font></b></u></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>SEPARATION
  AGREEMENT AND GENERAL RELEASE, by and between Public Service Enterprise Group
  Incorporated, a New Jersey Corporation, (the &#147;Company&#148;) and [ _________________
  ] (&#147;Executive&#148;), dated as of [ ______________ ], (&#147;this Agreement&#148;).</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, the Company maintains the Key Executive Severance Plan of Public Service Enterprise Group Incorporated (the &#147;Plan&#148;), effective December 20, 2004, and as thereafter amended, modified or supplemented;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, Executive was designated as an Eligible Employee under the Plan by the Organization and Compensation Committee of the Company&#146;s board of directors on December 19, 2004 and became a Participant in the Plan as of [date] ;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, the Company or one of its Affiliates terminated Executive&#146;s employment effective [date] (the &#147;Termination Date&#148;);</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, pursuant to Section 3.3 of the Plan, in order to be a Participant in and be entitled to benefits and protections under the Plan, Executive must execute and delivery this Agreement to the Company within forty-five days after Executive receives this Agreement; and</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>WHEREAS, Executive and the Company desire to settle fully and finally any differences, rights and duties arising between them, including, but in no way limited to, any differences, rights and duties that have arisen or might arise out of or are in any way related to Executive&#146;s employment with the Company, and the conclusion of that employment;</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>NOW THEREFORE, Executive and the Company agree as follows:</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>1.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Terms</font></u><font size=2>. All capitalized terms in this Agreement shall have the same meanings and definitions as assigned to such terms in the Plan.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>2.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Separation Payment</font></u><font size=2>. The Company acknowledges that the Executive is entitled to and that the Company will provide the payments and benefits described in Article IV of the Plan, all such payments and benefits to be paid to Executive less all applicable withholdings.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>3.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Release of Claims</font></u><font size=2>. Executive, for himself and for his children, heirs, administrators, representatives, executors, successors and assigns, releases and gives up any and all claims and rights which he has, may have or hereafter may have against the Company, its Affiliates and their respective subsidiaries, affiliates, predecessors, successors, assigns, officers, directors, shareholders, employees and agents and all of their predecessors, successors and assigns (the &#147;Releasees&#148;) from the beginning of the world until the date of the execution of this Agreement, including, but not limited to, any and all charges, complaints, claims, liabilities, obligations, promises, agreements, controversies, damages, remedies, actions, causes of action, suits, rights, demands, costs,
losses, debts and expenses (including attorneys&#146; fees and costs) of </font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'>&nbsp;</p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>any nature whatsoever, whether known or unknown, whether in law or equity (collectively, &#147;Claims&#148;), including, but not limited to, any Claims related to Executive&#146;s employment with the Company and the conclusion thereof, any Claims based on wrongful termination, any Claims based on contract whether express or implied, written or oral, and any Claims arising under the United States and/or State Constitutions, federal and/or common law, and/or rights arising out of alleged violations of any federal, state or other government statutes, regulations or ordinances including, without limitation, the National Labor Relations Act, Title VII of the 1964 Civil Rights Act, the Age Discrimination in Employment Act, the Older Workers&#146; Benefit Protection Act, the Sarbanes-Oxley Act, the New Jersey Law Against Discrimination, the New Jersey Conscientious Employee Protection Act, the Americans with Disabilities Act, the
Civil Rights Act of 1866 (42 U.S.C. &sect; 1981), the Civil Rights Act of 1991, the Equal Pay Act, the Family and Medical Leave Act, the Fair Labor Standards Act and the Employees Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, all as amended. This release specifically includes, but is not limited to, the right to the payment of wages, vacation, pension benefits or any other employee benefits, and any other rights arising under federal, state or local laws prohibiting discrimination and/or harassment on the basis of age, race, color, religion, creed, sex, national origin, ancestry, mental or physical disability, alienage or citizenship status, marital status, or any other basis prohibited by law.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>4.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Covenant Not To Sue</font></u><font size=2>. Executive has not filed against the Company or any of the Releasees, any complaints, charges or lawsuits with any government agency, arbitral tribunal, self-regulatory body, or any court arising out of Executive&#146;s employment by the Company or any other matter arising on or prior to the date hereof. Executive will not, directly or indirectly, commence or prosecute, or assist in the filing, commencement or prosecution in any court, arbitral tribunal, self-regulatory body or local or state government agency, any claim or charge against the Company or any of the Releasees arising out of any of the matters set forth in this Agreement or based upon any common law or statutory claim against the Company or any of the Releasees that can be brought under federal,
state or local law. Notwithstanding the foregoing, Executive shall not be limited from commencing a proceeding for the sole purpose of enforcing his rights under this Agreement or under the Plan, provided Executive first complies with the Claims Review procedures described in Article X of the Plan.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>5.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>No Admission of Liability</font></u><font size=2>. This Agreement does not constitute or imply an admission of liability or wrongdoing by Executive, the Company or any of the Releasees.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>6.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>No Disparagement</font></u><font size=2>. Executive and the officers and directors of the Company and its Affiliates agree that they will not make, or cause to be made, any statements, observations or opinions, or communicate any information (whether oral or written) that disparages or is likely in any way to harm the reputation in the case of the officers and directors of the Company and its Affiliates, Executive, and in the case of Executive, the Company, its Affiliates or any of the Releasees.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>7.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Confidentiality</font></u><font size=2>. The terms of this Agreement are </font><b><font SIZE=2>CONFIDENTIAL</font></b><font size=2>. Executive agrees not to tell anyone about this Agreement and not to disclose any information contained in this Agreement to anyone, other than to his lawyer, financial advisor or immediate family members, to enforce this Agreement, or to respond to a valid subpoena or other legal process. If Executive does tell his lawyer, financial advisor or immediate family members about this </font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>2</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>Agreement or its contents, he must immediately tell them that they must keep it confidential as well. The Company agrees that it will keep the terms of this Agreement confidential, except as is necessary to administer this Agreement, as required by law or to respond to a valid subpoena or other legal process.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>8.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>No Reliance</font></u><font size=2>. Executive represents that in executing this Agreement he does not rely and has not relied upon any representation or statement not set forth in this Agreement that the Company or any of its agents, representatives or attorneys may have made with regard to the subject matter, basis or effect of this Agreement.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>9.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Governing Law</font></u><font size=2>. This Agreement shall be construed in accordance with the laws of the State of New Jersey without regard to any state&#146;s conflict of law provisions.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>10.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Remedy for Breach</font></u><font size=2>. In the event of any breach of this Agreement, the parties may only institute an action for specific enforcement of the terms of this Agreement and the Plan and seek damages resulting from such breach. Executive may not institute any proceeding based on any Claims related to his employment with the Company or the conclusion of his employment because of a breach of this Agreement or the Plan by the Company. The prevailing party in any such action shall be entitled to an award of attorneys&#146; fees and costs in addition to any other legal or equitable relief, except that the Company will not be entitled to its attorneys&#146; fees or other damages if Executive challenges the validity or enforceability of this Agreement.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>11.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Severability</font></u><font size=2>. If at any time, after the date of the execution of this Agreement, any provision of this Agreement shall be held in any court or agency of competent jurisdiction to be illegal, void or unenforceable, such provision shall be of no force and effect. In the event that a court or agency of competent jurisdiction concludes that the release contained in paragraph 3 or the covenant not to sue contained in paragraph 4 are illegal, void or unenforceable, Executive agrees to execute a release and covenant not to sue that are legal, valid and enforceable.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>12.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Entire Agreement</font></u><font size=2>. This Agreement, the Plan and the Restrictive Covenant Agreement required by Section 3.2 of the Plan set forth the entire agreement between the parties with respect to the termination of Executive&#146;s employment and supersede any and all prior understandings and agreements between the parties. Neither party shall have any obligation toward the other except as set forth herein and therein.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>13.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Modifications</font></u><font size=2>. This Agreement may not be modified except in writing signed by all parties.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>14.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Enforceability</font></u><font size=2>. The parties are bound by this Agreement. Anyone who succeeds to the parties&#146; rights and responsibilities, such as their heirs, executors, successors or assigns, is also bound.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>15.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Headings</font></u><font size=2>. The headings contained in this Agreement are for the convenience of reference only and are not intended to define, limit, expand or describe the scope or intent of any provision of this Agreement.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>16.</font><font size=1>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><u><font size=2>Acknowledgements</font></u><font size=2>. Executive acknowledges that:</font></p>

<br><p style='margin-bottom:0pt;text-align:center'><font size=2>3</font></p>
<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2"><p style='page-break-before:always'></p><PAGE>

<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>b.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>Executive has been given forty-five (45) days to consider his rights and obligations under this Agreement and to consult with an attorney;</font></td></tr></table>
<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>c.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>The Company advised Executive to consult with an attorney and/or any other advisors of his choice before signing this Agreement;</font></td></tr></table>
<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>d.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>Executive understands that this Agreement is </font><b><font SIZE=2>LEGALLY BINDING </font></b><font size=2>and by signing it he gives up certain rights; </font></td></tr></table>
<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>e.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>Executive has voluntarily chosen to enter into this Agreement and has not been forced or pressured in any way to sign it; </font></td></tr></table>
<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>f.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>Executive </font><b><font SIZE=2>KNOWINGLY AND VOLUNTARILY RELEASES </font></b><font size=2>the Company and the Releasees from any and all claims Executive may have, known or unknown, in exchange for the benefits Executive has obtained by signing, and that these benefits are in addition to any benefit Executive would have otherwise received if he did not sign this Agreement;</font></td></tr></table>
<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>g.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>The General Release in this Agreement includes a </font><b><font SIZE=2>WAIVER OF ALL RIGHTS AND CLAIMS </font></b><font size=2>Executive may have under the Age Discrimination In Employment Act of 1967 (29 U.S.C. &sect;621 et seq.); and</font></td></tr></table>
<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0><tr><td width="8%" ></td><td width="4%" nowrap valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>h.</font></td><td valign="top"><p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:6pt;'><font size=2>Executive has seven (7) days after he signs this Agreement to revoke it by notifying the Company in writing. Executive must deliver the written revocation to the Company&#146;s General Counsel so that it is actually received by the Company within seven (7) days of the date Executive signs this Agreement. This Agreement will not become effective or enforceable until the Company receives a copy of this Agreement signed by Executive and the seven (7) day revocation period has expired without Executive revoking this Agreement.</font></td></tr></table>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0.36in; margin-top:8pt;'><font size=2>IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the parties have executed this Agreement as of the date first written above.</font></p>
<p style=' margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt;'><font size=2>&nbsp;</font></p>
