<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 8 &#150; INDEMNITY</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">8.1 Against Liability Arising form Nuclear Incident



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PS shall indemnify Exelon and its officers, directors, and employees
against any and all liability that any of them may incur as the result of or
arising out of a &#147;nuclear incident&#148; at or involving the PS Nuclear Facilities
or &#147;source material,&#148; &#147;waste material&#148; or &#147;special nuclear material&#148;
transported from those facilities for disposal or other disposition, subject to
the Owners Agreement, except to the extent that any such liability is the
result of the gross negligence or intentional misconduct or willful disregard
of the facts by Exelon in performing under this Agreement. (For purposes of
this article 8.1, the terms in quotations shall have meanings given to them in
the Atomic Energy Act, as amended, and the NRC&#146;s implementing regulations).

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">8.2 Against Conventional Liability



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8.2.1 Without limiting PS&#146;s obligations under Article&nbsp;8.1, PS shall
indemnify, defend and hold harmless Exelon and its employees, officers, and
directors against any and all conventional liability any of them may incur in
connection with the Agreement or the performance thereof for personal injury or
damage to or destruction of property (including property of PS) except to the
extent any such damage and liability as the result of the gross negligence or
intentional misconduct or willful disregard of the facts of Exelon in
performing under this Agreement, and except as provided in the Owners
Agreement.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8.2.2 Exelon shall indemnify PS and its employees, officers and directors
against any and all liability any of them may incur resulting from the willful
misconduct gross negligence or willful disregard of the facts of Exelon, its
employees, officers, directors or consultants in connection with this Agreement
or its performance.

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 9 &#150; INSURANCE</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">9.1 Insurance and Financial Protection to be Maintained by PS



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;At all times during performance of the Services by Exelon, PS shall
maintain or cause to be maintained in full force and effect the following
policies of insurance or other financial protection:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.1.1 Insurance for Workers&#146; Compensation, or qualified self insurance,
for its employees in accordance with the requirements applicable for each of
its employee&#146;s place of work in New Jersey:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.1.2 Employers&#146; Liability Insurance or self insurance:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.1.3 Nuclear and non-nuclear property damage insurance; including
protection for Exelon and its officers, directors and employees, for damage to
or destruction of the property of PS and its contractors that may be located at
the PS Nuclear Facilities; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.1.4 &#147;Financial protection&#148; against &#147;public liability&#148; in the event of a
&#147;nuclear incident,&#148; including nuclear liability insurance as required under
Atomic Energy Act, as amended, and the NRC&#146;s implementing regulations. If the
current requirements respecting the maintenance of nuclear liability insurance
and other forms of &#147;financial protection&#148; shall cease to be applicable, the
amount of required &#147;financial protection&#148; reduced, or the cap on &#147;public
liability&#148; arising out of a &#147;nuclear incident&#148; as established by the Atomic
Energy Act shall be increased or eliminated, PS shall continue to provide such
protection for Exelon, as is then customary in the nuclear industry, and
consistent with the Owners Agreement, against &#147;public liability&#148; in the event
of a nuclear incident to the extent available from commercial, industry and
governmental sources and customary in the United States. (For purposes of this
Article&nbsp;9.1.4, the terms in quotations shall have the meanings given to them in
the Atomic Energy Act, as amended, and the NRC&#146;s implementing regulations.)

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">9.2 Insurance to be Maintained by Exelon



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.2.1 At all times during performance of the services by Exelon, Exelon
shall maintain or cause to be maintained in full force and effect the following
policies of insurance:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.2.1.1 Insurance for Worker&#146;s Compensation, or qualified
self-insurance for its employees, in accordance with the requirements
applicable for each of its employee&#146;s place of work and New Jersey.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.2.1.2 Employer&#146;s Liability, or self-insurance;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 10 &#150; FORCE MAJEURE</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Parties shall be excused from their respective performance obligations
under this Agreement, and for any delay in the progress or completion thereof,
to the extent such performance was prevented or its progress or completion is
delayed due to an event or events of Force Majeure; provided, however, no Force
Majeure event shall be deemed to excuse either Party&#146;s obligation to make any
payment when due and payable to the other. The Party wishing to assert the
Force Majeure event as a defense must provide reasonable Notice to the other
Party that the event prevents or is delaying its performance and shall take
reasonable measures to overcome the effect of the event (except that resolution
of strikes or other labor disputes shall be solely at such Party&#146;s discretion).

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 11 &#150; TERMINATION</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">11.1 Termination Without Cause



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement shall terminate at the end of the Initial Term unless, by
no later than 180&nbsp;days prior to the end of the Initial Term the Parties agree
to an extended Agreement. If an extended Agreement is not executed as provided
pursuant to this Article&nbsp;11.1, the Parties shall work in good faith to provide
for the smooth and orderly replacement of Exelon personnel and transition of
responsibility and work in progress as provided in Article&nbsp;11.5

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">11.2 Termination With Cause



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without limiting other remedies as may be available under this Agreement,
PS may terminate this Agreement at any time if Exelon has failed to
substantially perform, keep, or fulfill any undertakings, obligations or
conditions set forth in this Agreement (&#147;Deficiencies&#148;), PS has provided Exelon
written notice of such Deficiencies and Exelon has failed to cure such
deficiencies within 30&nbsp;days of receipt of such notice. In the case of such a
termination, there shall be a transition period of up to 180&nbsp;days following the
termination date to provide for the smooth and orderly replacement of Exelon
personnel and transition of responsibility and work in progress.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">11.3 Merger Termination



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Either party may terminate this Agreement by giving 180&nbsp;days prior written
notice to the other in the event of termination of the Merger Agreement.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">11.4 Termination for Change in Law



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If either Party has failed to obtain or maintain any government approval
or permit, the receipt or maintenance of which is required for the lawful
performance of this Agreement, or if subsequent to the Effective Date hereof
there is a change in applicable federal, state or local laws, rules,
regulations or ordinances (and any judicial or administrative interpretation
thereof) that has the effect of imposing on either Party any materially
increased obligation, to or on a Party&#146;s performance or any requirement for a
Party to obtain or maintain any new, material governmental approval or permit,
then either Party may terminate this Agreement by providing written Notice to
the other Party, such Notice to state the circumstance(s) giving rise to the
right of termination.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Provided, however, a Party becoming aware of a circumstance that would
permit termination in accordance with this Article&nbsp;11.4 shall provide Notice of
termination within 60&nbsp;days after first becoming aware of such circumstance or
thereafter shall be barred from exercising a right of termination in accordance
with this Article&nbsp;11.4 based upon such circumstance(s). Termination in
accordance with this Article&nbsp;11.4 shall be effective 180&nbsp;days after the
non-terminating Party receives


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">21
</DIV>

<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2">
<p style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<PAGE>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">the Notice of Termination. During the period from the provision of the
Notice of termination, pursuant to this Article&nbsp;11.4, to the date of
termination, the Parties will negotiate in good faith to cure the adverse
effect that has caused the terminating Party to provide Notice of termination
and, if such negotiations are unsuccessful, the parties shall work in good
faith to provide for the smooth and orderly replacement of Exelon personnel and
transition of responsibility and work in progress as provided in Article&nbsp;11.5.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">11.5 Termination Transition



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the event a Notice of Termination is given pursuant Article&nbsp;11.1, 11.2
(and deficiencies are not cured), 11.3 or 11.4, Exelon shall continue to
provide, for a period of at least 180&nbsp;days and up to 2&nbsp;years, at the election
of PS, the full complement of personnel, services and Additional Services which
were being supplied prior to the Notice of Termination. (The &#147;Termination
Transition Period&#148;) Exelon shall cooperate fully with PS and provide
assistance in training and qualifying replacement personnel to assume
management responsibilities at the PS Nuclear Facilities during the Termination
Transition Period.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PS shall notify Exelon of the duration of the Termination Transition
Period with 90&nbsp;days of a Notice of Termination under Article&nbsp;11. If PS
determines that additional time is necessary to complete required activities
during the Termination Transition Period, such period shall be extended at the
election of PS for a period no more that 12&nbsp;months from the date the
Termination Transition Period would otherwise end, provided that PS gives
Exelon at least 90&nbsp;days notice of its intent to extend such Period prior to the
expiration of the Termination Transition Period.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;During the Termination Transition Period, including any extension, the
non-solicitation provision of the Confidentiality Agreement between Exelon and
PS dated August&nbsp;12, 2004 shall not apply to Exelon personnel providing On-Site
Operating Services, and PS may offer employment to these Exelon personnel.
Except as modified herein, all other terms of said Agreement shall remain in
full force. PS may identify additional Exelon personnel to which it wishes to
offer employment, and Exelon may, in its discretion, waive its non-solicitation
rights. Exelon agrees not to enter into or to waive any legally binding
arrangements with any such personnel which would have the effect of restricting
them from accepting employment with PS.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;During the Termination Transition Period, Exelon shall continue to receive
compensation and Payment in accordance with Article&nbsp;5 hereof.

</DIV>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">11.6 General



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Whether PS or Exelon provides notice of termination of the Agreement, or
the Agreement terminates pursuant to any of the provisions in this Article&nbsp;11,
PS shall be responsible for Exelon&#146;s reasonable costs for demobilization from
the PS Nuclear Facilities.

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 12 &#150; REPRESENTATIONS</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">12.1 Representations of Exelon



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.1.1 Exelon is a limited liability company duly formed, validly existing
and in good standing under the laws o the Commonwealth of Pennsylvania.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.1.2 Exelon is duly qualified to do business and in good standing as a
foreign corporation in New Jersey.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.1.3 The execution and delivery by Exelon of this Agreement and the
performance of its obligations under this Agreement have been duly and validly
authorized by all requisite corporate action. This Agreement has been duly
executed by Exelon and delivered to PS constitutes the legal, valid and binding
obligation of Exelon enforceable against it in accordance with its terms except
insofar as the enforceability thereof may be limited by applicable laws
regarding bankruptcy and creditors rights and general principles of equity.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.1.4 Exelon has obtained all those permits, authorizations and approvals
required to execute and deliver this Agreement and to perform its duties and
obligations under this Agreement.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.1.5 Exelon will select and assign to PS Nuclear Facilities individuals
for which it has reasonable basis to believe are qualified and capable of
fulfilling the roles to which they are assigned.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">12.2 Representations of PS



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.2.1 PS is a limited liability company duly formed, validly existing and
in good standing under the laws of the State of Delaware and is duly qualified
to do business and in good standing in New Jersey.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.2.2 The execution and delivery by PS of this Agreement and the
performance of PS obligations under this Agreement have been duly and validly
authorized by all requisite corporate action of PS. This Agreement has been
duly executed by PS and delivered to Exelon and constitutes the legal, valid
and binding obligation of PS enforceable against it in accordance with its
terms except insofar as its enforceability may be limited by applicable laws
regarding bankruptcy and creditors rights and general principles of equity.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12.2.3 PS has obtained all those permits, authorizations and approvals
required for PS to execute and deliver this Agreement and to perform their
duties and obligations under this Agreement.

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 13 &#150; NOTICES</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All Notices required to be given pursuant to this Agreement shall be in
writing, shall be (1)&nbsp;effective when received if delivered by hand, forwarded
by a nationally recognized commercial courier, sent by registered or certified
mail (return receipt requested, postage prepaid) or (2)&nbsp;effective upon sender&#146;s
receipt of telephonic confirmation if sent by telecopier. Notices shall be
addressed as follows:

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 14 &#150; CONFIDENTIALITY</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">In addition to the obligations of Section&nbsp;17.14, the terms of this Agreement
shall be treated by each of the Parties as Confidential Information which,
excepted as otherwise required by law, shall not be disclosed to any third
party without the express written consent of the Parties.

</DIV>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">




<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 15 &#150; BOOKS, DOCUMENTS, RECORDS AND AUDITS</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">15.1 Exelon shall maintain necessary books, documents and records of all costs
relating to work performed hereunder in order that all provisions of this
Agreement can be adequately administered. In so doing, Exelon shall use only
generally accepted accounting methods and practices and will notify PS of any
significant changes to such accounting methods and practices which are planned
prior to implementing the change.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">15.2 Upon reasonable notice. Exelon shall make available to PS, at the
location where such records are maintained, all relevant accounting and
financial books, documents and records as may be requested by PS to provide a
clear and adequate record of all payments requested by Exelon insofar as, and
only as they pertain to any invoice paid by PS, Exelon shall be solely
responsible to make available from any of its subcontractors or suppliers such
similar supporting documentation as PS may request.



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PS shall have the following rights to perform audits at its own expense:
such audit rights shall not be mutually exclusive and any audit performed under
one provision may be repeated, at the discretion of PS, under the other.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PS shall have the right, upon written advance notification to Exelon, to
audit relevant books, documents and records, as described in paragraph 15.1, of
Exelon and any contractor relating to any work performed under this contract.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PS shall have the right, upon written advance notification to Exelon to
have an audit as described above, performed by a recognized independent
auditing firm selected by PS.

</DIV>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 16 &#150; NRC COMPLIANCE</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exelon will conduct activities at the PS Nuclear Facilities in compliance
with applicable NRC requirements, including, without limitation, 10 CFR 50.7,
and will indemnify PS for actions taken by Exelon employees in violation of
such requirements where the action of Exelon constitutes gross negligence,
intentional misconduct or willful disregard of the facts by Exelon in
performing under this Agreement.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Work performed under this Agreement is subject to the provisions of 10 CFR
Part&nbsp;21. If assistance in evaluating potential deviations for reportability
under Part&nbsp;21 is required or if Exelon is to make any notification to the NRC
pursuant to Part&nbsp;21, notification shall be made to PS.

</DIV>

<PAGE>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ARTICLE 17 &#150; MISCELLANEOUS</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.1 Relationship to Owners Agreement



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as provided in Article&nbsp;5.12, nothing in this Agreement shall be
construed to amend or modify the rights and obligations of the Parties under
the Salem Owners Agreement.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.2 Amendments



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement may not be amended, altered, modified, or supplemented
except in a writing signed by the authorized representatives of each of the
Parties.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.3 Headings



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The headings in this Agreement are not be construed in interpreting this
Agreement or the intention of the Parties to this Agreement

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.4 Relationship of the Parties



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exelon shall at all times act as and be an independent contractor to PS.
This Agreement shall not constitute an agreement of employment with respect to
any of the personnel of Exelon assigned to provide Services under this
Agreement and shall not be so construed. PS shall not become the employer or
co-employee of any of Exelon&#146;s employees with respect to the Services. Exelon
shall bear the sole and entire liability to all its employees for all employee
benefits and worker compensation obligations owned to such employees.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.5 No Waivers



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A Party&#146;s consent to waiver of or acquiescence in prior conduct of the
other Party that breached or otherwise did not conform to the requirements of
this Agreement shall not be a bar or be raised as a defense, to such Party&#146;s
right to seek enforcement of this Agreement in accordance with its terms as
regards any subsequent or continuing conduct by the other Party that breaches
or otherwise does not conform to the requirements of this Agreement. The
giving of consent by a Party in one instance shall not limit or waive the
necessity to obtain such Party&#146;s consent in any future instance.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.6 Assignment/Delegation



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Neither Party shall assign its rights or obligations under this Agreement
to any person or entity not a Party hereto, without the prior written consent
of the other Party, which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld. The
duties and obligations of Exelon hereunder shall not be delegated or
subcontracted, in whole or in part, to any person or entity except where such
delegation or subcontract is approved in advance by PS.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">30
</DIV>

<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2">
<p style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<PAGE>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.7 Compliance with Laws



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exelon and its employees shall comply with all federal, state and local
laws and regulations applicable to the provision of Services under this
Agreement.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.8 Invalidity of Terms



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If any provision of this Agreement is illegal, invalid, or unenforceable
under present or future law effective during and applicable to this Agreement
or its performance, such provision shall be fully severable and this Agreement
shall, to the extent possible and without destroying the intent of the
Agreement, be construed as if such illegal, invalid or unenforceable provisions
had never been a part of this Agreement and the remaining provisions of this
Agreement shall remain in full force and effect.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.9 Separate Counterparts



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement may be signed by the representatives of the Parties in
separate counterparts, and the different counterparts signed by each of the
Parties, taken together, shall evidence the agreement of the Parties.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.10 Responsibility for Payment of Taxes



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Party shall be responsible for the payment of taxes imposed upon it
by law related to the provision or receipt of Services hereunder.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.11 Employee Security, Access and Exit Control



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exelon employees working under this Agreement must comply with all
requirements relating to Security, Access and Exit Control at the PS Nuclear
Facilities.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.12 Relationship of Staff Exchange Agreement



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement shall supersede the Staff Exchange Agreement between PS and
Exelon effective as of October&nbsp;1, 2004 to the extent that such Agreement
relates to Exelon Employees. Such Agreement shall remain in effect to the
extent it relates to PS employees.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.13 Confidentiality



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exelon and its employees and PS and its employees shall treat information
designated by either as Confidential and Proprietary, as confidential and shall
not disclose such information to any third party or to any other employee
(unless such employee need to know such information to perform assigned duties)
without the express written consent of Exelon or PS, as appropriate.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">31
</DIV>

<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2">
<p style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<PAGE>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Provided, however, that nothing contained herein shall prohibit or
restrict any such disclosure which is required by applicable statute or
regulation.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">17.14 Entire Agreement



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement and the attachments hereto, which are incorporated herein
by reference, constitute the entire agreement of the Parties with respect to
the subject matter hereof and supersede all prior and contemporaneous
understandings and agreements of the Parties respecting such subject matter.
The Parties intend that this Agreement should be interpreted in accordance with
the plain and unambiguous meanings of its provisions and that such
interpretation should not be affected or influenced by custom of usage of trade
or any course of dealings reflected by transactions between them that preceded
this Agreement.

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ATTACHMENT B &#150; RATE SCHEDULE</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">The Rate Schedule is based on average annual wages for each Salary Grade
Level multiplied by the burden for employee benefits, pension and
post-retiree benefits, payroll taxes and incentive. Actual billing will be
based on the assigned individual&#146;s hourly rate in accordance with Article
5.1. The Rate Schedule may be revised from time to time for changes in
Exelon compensation and benefits policies and escalation.

<PAGE>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>ATTACHMENT C &#150; REIMBURSABLE COSTS</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Reimbursable Costs for services provided under this Agreement are described
below.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Personnel Costs for On-Site Management</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Personnel providing On-Site Management Services will be reimbursed for
either (1)&nbsp;Relocation of primary residence or (2)&nbsp;Temporary Living Expense.
Exelon and its employees will make final determination of which option applies.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RELOCATION


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For personnel who relocate to the Salem Hope Creek area and choose to
purchase a home in the area, PSEG will reimburse Exelon for relocation expenses
made to the employee. Relocation reimbursement will include closing costs and
expenses associated with the sale of a primary residence, the move to the Salem
Hope Creek area and closing costs and expenses associated with the purchase of
a home in the area at the beginning of assignment. Reimbursement costs will
also include other incidental costs associated with relocation in accordance
with Exelon relocation policy.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;To allow personnel sufficient time to make a decision regarding
relocation, a period of 90&nbsp;days after reporting to Salem Hope Creek will be
designated. If they elect to relocate, a maximum of 120&nbsp;days will be allotted
to allow time for appraisal of their existing home, acceptance of the offer,
and time to vacate their home. Expenses for temporary living as described
below will apply during this transition period. Temporary living expenses would
be paid for a maximum of seven months or until the personnel move into their
new homes, whichever is earlier.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TEMPORARY LIVING EXPENSE


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Personnel who choose not to relocate their primary residence to the Salem
Hope Creek area will be reimbursed for temporary living allowance in accordance
with Exelon employee expense policies. Expenses will include but are not
limited to furnished lodging, basic utilities (electrical, telephone
installation, water, garage, sewer and housekeeping), leased vehicle or
reimbursement for personal vehicle use. A $25 per diem will be made for meals
and other small miscellaneous items to employees on Temporary Living Expense.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Employees who do not relocate and whose dependents remain in the primary
residence will be reimbursed for return trips to primary residence in
accordance with Exelon policies.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">36
</DIV>

<br><HR noshade align="center" width="100%" size="2">
<p style='page-break-before:always'></p>
<PAGE>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In lieu of temporary living expenses, Exelon may elect to pay its
employees a per diem to cover expenses. The per diem will be in accordance with
Exelon employee expense policy. The final determination of per diem or
temporary living expenses will be made by Exelon and its employees.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PSEG will reimburse Exelon for all temporary living expenses paid to
Exelon employees providing services under this Agreement.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Personnel Costs for Additional Services</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exelon will be reimbursed for reasonable and customary travel and lodging
expenses of Exelon employees and consultants who incur such expenses as the
result of travel incident to the performance of Additional Services. Typical
expenses include but are not limited to:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="10%" nowrap align="right">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Round trip airfare.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="10%" nowrap align="right">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Rental car or use of a personal vehicle at
the mileage rate specified by Exelon employee expense
policis.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="10%" nowrap align="right">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Meals, lodging, including hotel, motel or
rental property, as well as reimbursement for utilities
(telephone, electricity, gas, oil, etc.) where billed
separately.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

    <TD width="10%" nowrap align="right">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Other expenses, such as parking, tolls,
laundry services in accordance with Exelon policies.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Consultant Charges</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Reimbursable costs and actual charges without markup payable by Exelon to
its consultants related to the performance of the Services hereunder will be
reimbursed by PSEG.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Relocation Costs Upon Termination of Agreement or Assignment</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;At the end of the Agreement in accordance with Article&nbsp;2 or upon
termination pursuant to Article&nbsp;11, PSEG shall be responsible for relocation
costs for Exelon personnel providing On-Site Management Services, provided that
such personnel (a)&nbsp;have previously relocated their resident to Salem Hope Creek
area under the prevision of this Attachment and (b)&nbsp;are relocating back to work
at an Exelon facility. PSEG&#146;s responsibility for relocation costs shall also
apply if the relocation results from the Parties&#146; mutual agreement that an
individual&#146;s assignment is complete prior to termination of the Agreement.
Relocation costs hereunder would be provided consistent with the internal
policy of Exelon in effect at that time.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">37
</DIV>
